 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the ACM program manager, acm-pm@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

29. ANTC88H3S (2025 Winter) - Special Topics
Contemporary Colonialism and Palestine/Israel
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 How has Palestine become a country subject to intensive colonial dispossession and, according to many international authorities, now
subject to Israeli military genocide? And how does Palestine figure in an international system of imperialism and colonialism, where in particular
the strength of both the US and the State of Israel is brought to bear? This course explores these questions using historical and anthropological
studies in particular, as well as a variety of films, journalism, and other work. We will draw on examples of colonialism in the era of the nation-
state, and think of cases from other parts of the world that help us understand events in Palestine/Israel better. We will also explore how
protest movements around the world speak to the Question of Palestine.
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 WE 13:00 15:00 Available on ACORN 20 30 Y In-person Paz, A.
 Add to plan

49. BIOB98H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Introductory Research in Biology

Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a Supervised Study Form. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available
at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/biosci/undergraduate-research-opportunities
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email before the last day to add courses for the session. Staff will update your course
status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP)

80. BIOD95H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Study in Biology
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a Supervised Study Form. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study Form and Departmental
Permission Forms are available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/biosci/undergraduate-research-opportunities
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email before the last day to add courses for the session. Staff
will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

BBA degree requirements and is not included in your cGPA. There are no tuition fees attached to this course. AYCE will begin the first week of
classes.
For any questions regarding this class, please contact the Management Co-op Office at 416-287-7111 or mgmtcoop.utsc@utoronto.ca

on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to Kelly Squier
kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved (APP). The Supervised Study form
is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

190. EESC24H3S (2025 Winter) - Advanced Readings in Environmental Science
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Contact the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form . Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and any additional paperwork by email to dpes-undergrad.utsc@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Physical and Environmental Science Office EV243
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes

196. EESD09H3S (2025 Winter) - Research Project in Environmental Science
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Contact the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form . Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and any additional paperwork by email to dpes-undergrad.utsc@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Physical and Environmental Science Office EV243

252. FRED02H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Reading
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Secure a faculty member you would be interested in working with as a supervisor for your project.
Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title

of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the departmental office listed for more information.
Step 4: Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-da@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Department of Language Studies Office MW304

Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title

of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Arifa Nitol arifa.nitol@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

283. GGRD12H3S (2025 Winter) - Seminar in Selected Topics in Human Geography
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Topic: Doing Relational Geography
Course Description: In A Treaty Guide for Torontonians, co-authors write that engaging with and learning about treaty relations will "deepen
our understanding of the agreements that underpin relationships between our peoples here - as well as the responsibilities [that] these
relationships entail for all Torontonians, Indigenous and non-Indigenous" (2022, 6). This course connects what geographers might call 'vitalist
ontologies' and 'new materialism' with Indigenous-led approaches to relationality. In so doing, we attend to concepts and practices including
relational ontologies, 'more-than-human' agency, becoming kin, solidarity, the sacred, and world-making. Teaching and learning will be
grounded in the practice of making ethical space across difference on Indigenous lands (Ermine 2007) and critical of the racial logics that
inform contemporary hierarchies of being (Sundberg 2024; King 2019). The seminar course will involve reading and discussion, experimentation
with embodied and land-based learning, and the exploration of learning outputs that contribute meaningfully to public education.
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 WE 11:00 13:00 Available on ACORN 8 20 Y In-person Latulippe, N.
 Add to plan

288. GGRD49H3S (2025 Winter) - Land and Land Conflicts in the America
Enrolment Indicator: P
Initially restricted to students in the following groups:
SCSPECIT - Specialist Program in City Studies
SCMAJCIT - Major Program in City Studies
SCMAJCIT C - Major (Co-operative) Program in City Studies
SCMIN1810 - Minor Program in City Studies (Arts)
SCSPE1666H - Specialist Program in Human Geography
SCMAJ1666H - Major Program in Human Geography
SCMIN1666H - Minor Program in Human Geography
SCMAJ1666P - Major Program in Physical and Human Geography
Enrolment will open to all UTSC students at 10:00 am on July 24, 2024. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Course Description: This course explores various ways of making claims to possess, or use land by first unsettling common-sense ideas
about ownership and then tracing these through examples of classed, gendered and racialized property regimes. Through this exploration, the
course shows that claims to land are historically and geographically specific, and structured by colonialism, and capitalism. Informed by a
feminist interpretation of “conflict,” we look at microprocesses that scale up to largescale transformations in how land is lived. We end by
engaging with Black and Indigenous epistemologies regarding how land might be differently cared for and occupied.

LEC01 TH 13:00 15:00 Available on ACORN 12 20 Y In-person Goffe, R.

307. HISD01H3S (2025 Winter) - Independent Studies: Senior Research Project
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to hcs-uc@utsc.utoronto.ca. Staff will update your course
status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes

SCMAJ2085K - Major (Co-operative) Program in Health Studies - Population Health Stream (Science)
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Secure a faculty member as a supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Ensure the course code, supervisor's
name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is
available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.

Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Sean Ramrattan sean.ramrattan@utoronto.ca one week prior to the last day to
add courses for the session. Staff will ensure your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

344. IDSB02H3S (2025 Winter) - Development and Environment
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Course description: This course will examine the interface between development and the environment in a global context. The specific aims
of the course are to:
1. Examine the fundamental physical and biological principles of key environmental problems associated with international development.
2. Provide an introduction to the central issues and debates associated with development and environmental change.
3. Develop an understanding of the environmental limits on human activities.
4. Develop research, writing, and critical analysis skills necessary for success at the undergraduate level.
Upon completion of this course, students will be able to appreciate the complex interactions between ecological and biophysical processes,
and socioeconomics of development. Students will be able to identify and assess the multiple political and economic actors and factors
contributing to environmental change, and the social consequences of these changes. Finally, students will be able to discuss and critique the
current sustainable development debates and initiatives.

350. IDSC15H3S (2025 Winter) - Topics in International Development Studies
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled

 Topic: Critical Approaches to Studying Youth and Children in International Development
Course Description: This interdisciplinary course examines key concepts, theories, and ideas around youth and children in international
development. We will consider the ways in which youth and children’s lived experiences are often shaped by social, political, and economic
factors outside of their own control as well as the different social locations in which they are situated. In this course, race, gender, sex, class, and
disability will all be relevant in exploring questions of both the rights of children and youth as well as ethical responsibilities to them at global
and local levels. We will also examine how personhood has been defined historically, and the way its meaning has changed over time to shape
the lives of children and youth. As part of this course, students will learn how the UN’s Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) attend to the
specific issues shaping the development and well-being of youth and children. This course will run as a seminar with interactive lectures, class
discussions, audiovisual technologies, and case studies. Class materials will draw from research articles, social media, online resources, blogs,
and print media, to center the lives of youth and children in the context of international development.
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 TU 11:00 13:00 Available on ACORN 40 40 Y In-person Ilmi, A.
 Add to plan

be updated within 10 days of this notification.

[7] Students whose level of proficiency in the language is considered unsuitable for the course will not be permitted to take the course.

course). Click a specific course code to read the description, including the Exclusion.

 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Secure a faculty member you would be interested in working with as a supervisor for your project.
Step 2: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 3: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the departmental office listed for more information.
Step 4: Submit the fully completed and signed Supervised Study form by email to dls-da@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Department of Language Studies Office MW304

420. MATD12H3S (2025 Winter) - Topics in Mathematics
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Permission of instructor is required.

MATD02H3, MATC27H3, and MATD67H3 will be the required prerequisites for this course offering.
"MATD12 (3-Manifolds) serves as a natural continuation of the Classical Plane Geometries and their Transformations (MATD02). In this course,
we aim to cover a selection of the following topics: Topological Manifolds, Differentiable Manifolds, Oriented Manifolds, Triangulated
Manifolds, Geometric Manifolds, Connected Sums, Equivalence of Categories, Classification of Surfaces, Decompositions of Surfaces, Covering
Spaces and Branched Covering Spaces, Homotopy and Isotopy on Surfaces, The Mapping Class Group, 3-Manifold Bundles, The Schönflies
Theorem, Incompressible Surfaces, Knots and Links in 3-Manifolds."

Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input
on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to Kelly Squier
kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved (APP). The Supervised Study form
is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

493. MGED90H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Reading
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGE faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their approval. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study form as this information will appear on your transcript. The
Supervised Study form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to the Academic
Director, Economics ecoss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar’s Office with your Supervised Study form. Staff will update your
course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Policy%20on%20Supervised%20Reading%20Cou
rses%20(October%202023).pdf
Economics and Management Office IC250

Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 Available on ACORN 0 9999 Y In-person

do so.
Students are expected to enroll or waitlist for course meeting sections that fit in a conflict-free schedule. Students who knowingly enroll in a

505. MGFD85H3S (2025 Winter) - Advanced Special Topics in Finance
Enrolment Indicator: R
Restricted to students in the following groups:
MGT - All Management Students
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Visiting students require the permission of the Academic Director.
Course Topic: Fixed Income Securities
Course Description:
This course provides an in-depth understanding of fixed-income securities and their role in financial markets. Students will learn about the
institutional details of bond markets, bond valuation concepts, and the determinants of short- and long-term interest rates. They will also gain
knowledge of term structure models with binomial trees, the Vasicek model, Monte Carlo simulations, and pricing of defaultable bonds.
Additionally, the course will cover the relationships between interest rates and the macroeconomy, and develop the communication skills
necessary to present complex financial concepts. This course is ideal for students interested in pursuing a career in finance or banking, as it
provides a solid foundation in the essential concepts and tools used in the fixed-income market.
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 TU 09:00 11:00 Available on ACORN 33 42 Y In-person Nozawa, Y.
 Add to plan

540. MGTD80H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Reading in Management
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGE faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and obtain their approval. Make sure the course
code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the supervised study form as this information will appear on your transcript. The
Supervised Study form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form .
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to the Academic
Director, Economics ecoss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your Supervised Study form. Staff will update your
course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.
Economics and Management Office IC250
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 Available on ACORN 1 9999 Y In-person

 Course enrolment in the following Music Performance course is by an interview. An interview sign-up sheet will be sent to students closer to
the beginning of an academic term. To be considered follow the steps below:
* Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be 'INT'.
* Attend a placement interview - normally held during the week before and during the first week of classes. For more details please visit
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/acm/music-culture and view the FAQ link.
* Decisions will be updated on ACORN beginning Monday, September 9th for the Fall Term and Monday, January 13th for the Winter term.
Please enrol in a course you have the prerequisite for. Approval will only be granted if student is enrolled in the correct course.
Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. If ACORN has not been updated contact the Instructor
immediately.

572. MUZD81H3S (2025 Winter) - Independent Study in Music

Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Music Program Director to obtain permission to enroll in this course. You will be asked to choose a supervisor and then
obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on
the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Students should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the ACM program manager, acm-pm@utsc.utoronto.ca
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

598. PHLC45H3S (2025 Winter) - Advanced Topics in Philosophy
Open to all UTSC students. Enrolment will open to UTSG and UTM students on August 2, 2024.
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 Subtitle: “Philosophy and Race”
Course Description: This course will begin by asking “what, exactly, is race?” Is it a biological category? A social category? A metaphysical
category? Students will be presented with a number of historical and contemporary answers to this question. Subsequently, students will be
introduced to the aesthetics of race. We will ask, “is race an aesthetic project?” and “how can art subvert racist prejudices?” In the last section of the

course, students will be introduced to some of the political problems of race. This section will concern questions like: “in what way do slurs harm?”;
“when are reparations justified?”, and “what does it mean to say that capitalism causes racism?”
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 WE 12:00 15:00 Available on ACORN 19 35 Y In-person Hamblin, C.
 Add to plan

604. PHLD90H3S (2025 Winter) - Independent Study
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Please submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Jason Ferreira jason.ferreira@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Philosophy Department - MW374

623. PHYD01H3S (2025 Winter) - Research Project in Physics and Astrophysics
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
In order to qualify for a Supervised Study course, students must locate a professor who will agree to supervise the course, and then follow the
steps outlined below.
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be interim (INT).
You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps.
Step 2: Fill the 'Student' section on a 'Supervised Study Form' available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once you fill-in the 'Student' section, contact your Supervisor and provide them with the form. Your supervisor will complete their
section and forward the form for departmental approval.
Step 4: Once the project is approved at the departmental level, the form will be submitted to the Registrar's Office and your status on ACORN
will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 Available on ACORN 2 10 N In-person Weaver, D.

666. POLD95H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Research
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Marishka Pereira marishka.pereira@utoronto.ca.
The Department will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Political Science Office HL226

Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name and title
of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the Office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Marishka Pereira marishka.pereira@utoronto.ca.
The Department will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

728. SOCD40H3S (2025 Winter) - Supervised Independent Research
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Ensure the course code, supervisor's name and title of
the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. Students
should contact the office listed for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the Program Advisor

sociologyadvisor.utsc@utoronto.ca.
Your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Sociology Office HL206

745. STAD92H3S (2025 Winter) - Readings in Statistics
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input
on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to Kelly Squier
kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved (APP). The Supervised Study form
is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is input
on the form as this information will appear on your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised Study form by email to Kelly Squier
kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT) to approved (APP). The Supervised Study form
is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork.

809. WSTD01H3S (2025 Winter) - Independent Project in Womens and Gender Studies
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been granted. Check your status through ACORN to
see whether you have been approved. (APP = approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
 P = Priority, R = Restricted, A = Approval , E = Enrolment on ACORN is disabled
 SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until you complete the remaining steps
(below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and
title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department may require additional paperwork. Students should contact
the Office for more information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to hcs-psc@utsc.utoronto.ca. Staff will update your
course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Meeting Section Day(s) Start(s) End Location Current Max Wait Delivery Mode Instructor Notes
LEC01 Available on ACORN 0 9999 Y In-person
